3749	but this is not what we shall be doing when life is worth living again
3750	a wave of admiration almost of worship flowed out from winston towards obrien
3751	for the moment he had forgotten the shadowy figure of goldstein
3752	when you looked at obriens powerful shoulders and his bluntfeatured face so ugly and yet so civilized it was impossible to believe that he could be defeated
3753	there was no stratagem that he was not equal to no danger that he could not foresee
3754	even julia seemed to be impressed
3755	she had let her cigarette go out and was listening intently
3756	obrien went on
3757	you will have heard rumours of the existence of the brotherhood
3758	no doubt you have formed your own picture of it
3759	you have imagined probably a huge underworld of conspirators meeting secretly in cellars scribbling messages on walls recognizing one another by codewords or by special movements of the hand
3760	nothing of the kind exists
3761	the members of the brotherhood have no way of recognizing one another and it is impossible for any one member to be aware of the identity of more than a few others
3762	goldstein himself if he fell into the hands of the thought police could not give them a complete list of members or any information that would lead them to a complete list
3763	no such list exists
3764	the brotherhood cannot be wiped out because it is not an organization in the ordinary sense
3765	nothing holds it together except an idea which is indestructible
3766	you will never have anything to sustain you except the idea
3767	you will get no comradeship and no encouragement
3768	when finally you are caught you will get no help
3769	we never help our members
3770	at most when it is absolutely necessary that someone should be silenced we are occasionally able to smuggle a razor blade into a prisoners cell
3771	you will have to get used to living without results and without hope
3772	you will work for a while you will be caught you will confess and then you will die
3773	those are the only results that you will ever see
3774	there is no possibility that any perceptible change will happen within our own lifetime
3775	we are the dead
3776	our only true life is in the future
3777	we shall take part in it as handfuls of dust and splinters of bone
3778	but how far away that future may be there is no knowing
3779	it might be a thousand years
3780	at present nothing is possible except to extend the area of sanity little by little
3781	we cannot act collectively
3782	we can only spread our knowledge outwards from individual to individual generation after generation
3783	in the face of the thought police there is no other way
3784	he halted and looked for the third time at his wristwatch

3794	to the future
3795	to the past said winston
3796	the past is more important agreed obrien gravely
